<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">lantschap</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*lantskap</i>. <a href = vnd.unilang:equivalent.html>Equivalent</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:land.html>land</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-schap</i>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:langnekken.html>langnekken</a> (81926)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun"><a href = vnd.unilang:noun.html>Noun</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:langnekken.html>langnekken</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="use-with-mention">Plural <a href = vnd.unilang:form.html>form</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:langnek.html>langnek</a></i></span></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*laizō</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*laizijaną</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:teach.html>teach</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate <a href = vnd.unilang:with.html>with</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Saxon" class="extiw" title="w:Old Saxon"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:saxon.html>Saxon</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="osx">lēra</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language"><a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:leer.html>leer</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:high.html>High</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:german.html>German</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">lēra</i> (<span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language"><a href = vnd.unilang:german.html>German</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Lehre</i>).

<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it"><a href = vnd.unilang:lasagna.html>lasagna</a></i> (<a href = vnd.unilang:and.html>and</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:its.html>its</a> plural <i class="Latn mention" lang="it"><a href = vnd.unilang:latin.html>Latin</a> *<i>lasania</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin"><a href = href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek"><a href = vnd.unilang:ancient.html>Ancient</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:greek.html>Greek</a></a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">λάσανον</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lásanon</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">trivet <a href = vnd.unilang:or.html>or</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:stand.html>stand</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:for.html>for</a> <a <ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>A</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:flat.html>flat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:sheet.html>sheet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:pasta.html>pasta</a>.</li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:lass.html>lass</a> (35920)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:high.html>High</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:german.html>German</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">*<a href = vnd.unilang:los.html>los</a></i>, <a href = class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:loose.html>loose</a>; <a href = vnd.unilang:free.html>free</a>; lacking; <a href = vnd.unilang:sly.html>sly</a>, deceitful</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. <a href = vnd.unilang:compare.html>Compare</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:for.html>for</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:short.html>short</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vowel.html>vowel</a> Ripuarian <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Central_Franconian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Central Franconian language"><a href = vnd.unilang:central.html>Central</a> Franconian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmw-cfr"><a href = vnd.unilang:loss.html>loss</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language"><a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:los.html>los</a></i>. <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>The</a> uninflected <a href = vnd.unilang:stem.html>stem</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:this.html>this</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:adjective.html>adjective</a> develops <a href = vnd.unilang:regularly.html>regularly</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:into.html>into</a> Luxembourgish <i class="Latn mention" lang="lb"><a href = vnd.unilang:lass.html>lass</a></i>, <a href = lang="lb">lues</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:slow.html>slow</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:quiet.html>quiet</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. <a href = vnd.unilang:see.html>See</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:english.html>English</a> cognate <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:loose.html>loose</a></i> <a href =
